              * * *  Maple Integration Test Results - 2011-06-08  * * *


Test file:  AlgebraicFunctions/AlgebraicFunctionsOfLinears.txt

Valid but unnecessarily complicated antiderivative:
  Integrand        = (c*(a+b*x)^2)^(5/2)
  Optimal integral = 1/6*(a+b*x)*(c*(a+b*x)^2)^(5/2)/b
  Maple integral   = 1/6*x*(6*a^5+15*a^4*b*x+20*a^3*b^2*x^2+15*a^2*b^3*x^3+6*a*b^4*x^4+b^5*x^5)*(c*(a+b*x)^2)^(5/2)/(a+b*x)^5
  Leafcounts = 25 76   25 76

Valid but unnecessarily complicated antiderivative:
  Integrand        = (c*(a+b*x)^2)^(3/2)
  Optimal integral = 1/4*(a+b*x)*(c*(a+b*x)^2)^(3/2)/b
  Maple integral   = 1/4*x*(4*a^3+6*a^2*b*x+4*a*b^2*x^2+b^3*x^3)*(c*(a+b*x)^2)^(3/2)/(a+b*x)^3
  Leafcounts = 25 54   25 54

Valid but unnecessarily complicated antiderivative:
  Integrand        = 1/(c/(a+b*x)^2)^(3/2)
  Optimal integral = 1/4*(a+b*x)/b/(c/(a+b*x)^2)^(3/2)
  Maple integral   = 1/4*x*(4*a^3+6*a^2*b*x+4*a*b^2*x^2+b^3*x^3)/(a+b*x)^3/(c/(a+b*x)^2)^(3/2)
  Leafcounts = 25 54   25 54

Valid but unnecessarily complicated antiderivative:
  Integrand        = 1/(c/(a+b*x)^2)^(5/2)
  Optimal integral = 1/6*(a+b*x)/b/(c/(a+b*x)^2)^(5/2)

Incorrect antiderivative:

Valid but unnecessarily complicated antiderivative:
